### 1. 爆炸披萨切片动画和图像生成提示

**Author**: [AGAFE](https://x.com/tussiwe)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一组包含三个提示：一个用于生成运动（爆炸物体结构动画），另外两个用于生成超逼真的披萨切片图像，其中一个为标准图像，另一个为垂直信息图，均适用于高质量食品商业美学。

```
Motion Prompt:
The pizza slice rotates slowly in place, then smoothly separates into vertical layers. Each ingredient lifts upward in sequence while maintaining natural proportions and alignment. Motion is steady and realistic, with gentle floating and no extra visual effects.

Image 1 :-
A high-quality, professional food photograph of a single slice of {argument name="pizza type" default="Domino’s-style pepperoni pizza"}. Golden melted cheese with visible stretch, glossy pepperoni slices on top, thick crust with baked texture. Shot against a clean white background with soft shadows, studio food photography, sharp focus, ultra-realistic textures, 8K resolution.

Image 2 :-
Create a hyper-realistic exploded vertical infographic composition of a Domino’s pizza slice. At the top, slightly curled pepperoni slices with oil sheen. Below, a thick layer of melted mozzarella cheese stretching naturally. Underneath, a smooth red tomato sauce layer with visible herbs. Below that, a baked pizza dough base showing airy crumb texture and crust edge. Pure white background, soft studio lighting, subtle shadows beneath each floating layer, ultra-sharp focus, clean infographic text labels with thin pointer lines, premium fast-food commercial aesthetic, DSLR macro food photography, 8K quality.
```

light passing through ears and fingertips creating a red-orange internal glow", "global_illumination": "Warm bounce light from the gold embroidery reflecting onto the chin and jawline", "light_modifiers": "Diffusion silk to soften highlights on the forehead and nose", "color_temperature_k": "3200K (Warm interior glow)", "volumetric_lighting": "Subtle Bloom around the earring highlights", "specular_highlights": "Oil sheen on the T-zone and moisture glint in the axilla and midriff" } }, "composition_and_framing": { "aspect_ratio": "9:16 (Social/Mobile)", "camera_angles": "Chest-level, slightly low-angle to emphasize the powerful physique", "framing_technique": "Intimate close-up; hands behind head framing the face", "subject_geometry": "Central symmetry with leading curves of the raised arms", "background_depth": "Layered focus: sharp subject, soft-blurred warm architectural background" }, "subject_physiometry": { "demographics_and_build": { "age_estimate": "29-30 years old", "ethnicity_specifics": "South Indian (Malayali), warm olive skin undertones, thick dark hair, recognizable facial geometry of Nivetha Thomas", "body_type_category": "Soft-curvy, fuller/meaty build (2024 era)", "anthropometric_ratios": "Strong biacromial width; ### 16. 分解图玉米饼可视化和商业食品摄影提示

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的多部分提示，用于生成两张不同的图像和一个与玉米饼（taco）相关的动态序列。第一张图像是玉米饼的高端商业摄影，第二张是其配料的超现实分解图信息图，并有特定的注释设计要求。动态提示描述了用于视频生成的配料平滑分离过程。

![分解图玉米饼可视化和商业食品摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544778654_v0bebh_G-s-O_waMAAh7fH.jpg)

```
Motion Prompt: The food start to round spin while ingredients separate gently and precisely, maintaining alignment and scale. The motion is smooth, with no extra effects.

Image 1: A high-end commercial food photograph of the same two tacos from the reference image, preserving their exact structure, fillings, proportions, and arrangement. The camera angle is slightly adjusted to a more flattering three-quarter close-up, enhancing depth and appetite appeal without altering the tacos themselves. Soft cinematic lighting highlights the textures of the tortillas and fillings, with subtle steam and natural sheen to emphasize freshness. The background is replaced with a clean, modern, out-of-focus setting in warm complementary tones that enhance the food without distracting from it. Shallow depth of field, crisp focus on the tacos, rich contrast, natural colors, and premium restaurant advertising quality. No added or removed ingredients, refined composition, lighting, and environment.

Image 2: Exploded-view commercial visualization of the taco from the image, presented as premium recipe-style breakdown.

The taco is deconstructed into four visible ingredients, matching the original taco precisely in composition, color, and texture. No additional ingredients.

The ingredients are separated and arranged in a clean vertical stack, evenly spaced from bottom to top, floating in place with precise alignment and symmetry.

Ingredient order (bottom → top):

Soft wheat taco tortilla

Shredded red cabbage

Grilled chicken pieces

Sauce with garnish (topped with a small mixed garnish of diced onion, tomato, and parsley, approximately 5–6 small cubes total, lightly mixed, placed naturally on top)

Each ingredient is visually distinct and clearly readable in shape and texture.

Annotation design requirements:

– Large, bold sans-serif font, high legibility at feed scale

– Each annotation placed inside a solid or softly rounded rectangular color block

– Background color of each block corresponds subtly to the ingredient color (tomato red, lettuce green, meat warm brown, sauce white/cream, pita beige)

– High contrast text (dark on light, light on dark)

– Thick, clean connector lines pointing clearly to each ingredient

– No transparency that reduces readability

– Annotations must visually dominate over background without covering ingredients

Background is soft, neutral, and atmospheric, with subtle depth and gentle gradients, inspired by premium food advertising.

Overall style is clean, modern, and appetizing, commercial-ready without technical or schematic feel.

No extra elements, no substitutions, no reinterpretation of ingredients.
```

[[Commercial Food Photography]]

### 32. 洛杉矶屋顶泳池边自拍提示（女性主题）

**Author**: [gemini_prompts](https://x.com/YeKyaHoRhaHaiBe)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 以下是三组不同的照片级写实肖像提示词。提示词 1 侧重于波西米亚浪漫风格，搭配钩针服装和柔和的灯光。提示词 2 是高对比度的街头肖像，具有正午刺眼的阳光和胶片模拟效果。提示词 3 是一个女孩与小猫的柔和、富有氛围感的肖像，强调触感和微妙的运动模糊，需要一张参考图像来确定面部特征。

![三种超逼真肖像提示词（波西米亚风、街头风、柔和风）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544825302_z9tnwa_G-rgSUqbQAEzNpx.jpg)
![三种超逼真肖像提示词（波西米亚风、街头风、柔和风）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544825321_3zxfd2_G-rgSW5a0AAWmq0.jpg)
![三种超逼真肖像提示词（波西米亚风、街头风、柔和风）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544825324_3m0fqm_G-rgSUmbQAQdU8E.jpg)

```
Prompt 1:
"Generate an artistic close-up of a woman with a delicate appearance, light brown skin with warm tones, dark brown eyes and serene, seductive expression. She has long black hair, naturally wavy and slightly disheveled, falling over her shoulders. She's wearing a sophisticated crochet outfit, boho romantic style: light pink strapless top with colorful three-dimensional floral applications (orange, pink, blue, yellow) on the bust, loose sleeves in lace crochet and matching skirt with applied flowers. Gold flower-shaped earrings, in pastel tones. A pose using your hands. Background with textured pink wall, creating a vintage and poetic atmosphere. Soft, diffused lighting, natural light, enhancing the texture of skin and fabrics. Fashion editorial style, high resolution, shallow depth of field, sharp focus on face, smooth and harmonic colors, romantic aesthetic, boho chic, spring, professional photography, ultra-detailed. Generates a Realistic Photo. Lighting/Lighting: Soft, diffused sunlight, golden hour; Face highlight with soft shadows and realistic depth in 8K HDR. Framing / Framing: 9:16 vertical, focus on face and upper body, swap-ready for perfect facial replacement. Do not change my face."

Prompt 2:
"Hyper-realistic 8K street portrait, preserve the girl’s facial features from the reference. Stylish outdoor shot: girl leaning back against a textured beige stucco wall under bright sun, relaxed contrapposto stance, head tilted back, eyes half-closed, expression enjoying warmth. Wearing a trendy sage-mint set: twisted-knot long-sleeve crop top, exposed midriff, mini skirt with thong-strap detail on waist. Sunkissed makeup: bronzer, strong highlighter, nude matte lips, defined contoured cheekbone . Hair in messy bun with loose wavy face-framing strands. Background: rough stucco wall with sharp botanical shadows cast by leaves. Camera: Fujifilm X-T4, Kodak Gold 200 film emulation, high aperture f/8 for background sharpness. Lighting: harsh mid-day sun, high contrast light–shadow pattern, crisp plant shadows across skin and wall. Warm yellow-green tones, summer vibe, high clarity, magazine aesthetic. Medium shot composition, textured wall filling the frame. --ar 4:5 --style raw --v 6.0"

Prompt 3:
"Use the uploaded image as a reference for the character. Create a sweet, cute, youthful-looking girl with a relaxed, languid posture and expressive emotions.
She is holding her pet perisan kitten, She is surrounded by many green plants. The image should feel tactile, immersive, and atmospheric, with a sense of surreal sophistication and subtle motion blur. The girl has soft black hair styled naturally, with an asymmetrical composition, glancing left and right,and her hairstyle should enhance the mood. Her makeup is sweet and natural, facial features delicate and realistic.
Lighting should be soft, warm and a lamp orange bulb behind her creates softly oran
```

**Author**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: ja

> 以下是两个相关的提示（A 和 B），用于生成一个角色从放置在桌上的智能手机中动态出现，且超逼真的图像。两者都使用超广角和强制透视来夸大离镜头最近的手和脸的尺寸，从而营造出 3D 弹出效果。

![人物从智能手机屏幕中浮现（强制透视）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468602600_n8jbqp_G-oKQo7aoAExHwD.jpg)
![人物从智能手机屏幕中浮现（强制透视）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468602511_49ec7v_G-oKQoiaYAEJ_dV.jpg)
![人物从智能手机屏幕中浮现（强制透视）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468602575_xymxl4_G-oKQrra0AA4YPi.jpg)
![人物从智能手机屏幕中浮现（强制透视）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468603599_megt35_G-oKQrKaMAA5B4G.jpg)

```
🍌プロンプトA
超リアルな実写写真。テーブルの上に置かれたスマホから、このキャラクターが立体的に出てきた瞬間。片方の手はこちらに伸ばし、片手をスマホのフレームにかけ、下半身はスマホの中にあり足元は見切れている。キャラクターはこちらを見つめている。
強い誇張パース（extreme wide-angle, forced perspective）により、
手と顔がカメラのすぐ近くにあり極端に大きく見え、
下半身は奥に小さく見える立体的な奥行き構成。

🍌プロンプトB
超リアルな実写写真。テーブルの上に置かれたスマホから、このキャラクターが立体的に出てきた瞬間。片方の手はこちらに伸ばし、片足をスマホのフレームにかけ、下半身はスマホの中にある。大袈裟な遠近感で近くにある顔と手が大きく見える。参考画像の雰囲気から連想されるモチーフが一緒に飛び出てくる。キャラクターはこちらを見ながら勢いよく飛び出て、モーションブラーが発生している。
```

[[Forced Perspective]] [[Mixed Reality]]

```
{
  "scene_type": "Indoor lifestyle portrait",
  "environment": {
    "location": "Sunlit bedroom filled with soft natural daylight",
    "background": {
      "bed": "White metal-frame bed dressed with delicate floral-patterned bedding",

### 107. 角色便当产品图

**Author**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度详细的提示，用于生成“角色便当”（以角色为主题的午餐盒）的逼真产品照片，强调商业包装设计、食物真实感、特定构图（平铺拍摄），以及使用食物来表现角色特征。

![角色便当产品图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468609460_hkiqa6_G-nXMVFbAAAme_u.jpg)
![角色便当产品图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468609470_ep2pee_G-nXMVNaQAA2ONa.jpg)
![角色便当产品图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468609822_u7yu1a_G-nXMPQbIAAusLD.jpg)
![角色便当产品图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468610114_h7arj6_G-nXMUHbIAEAUgT.jpg)

```
キャラクター名：
（シーン・瞬間）
売り物としてパッケージされたキャラ弁風弁当の蓋が開けられ瞬間を捉えた一枚。

透明または紙製の蓋が弁当を隠さない程度に被されていて、中身が現れた瞬間。

（パッケージ・蓋の表現）
蓋の外側には、参考画像のキャラクターをモチーフにした商用向けパッケージデザインが印刷されている。参考画像を誇張した様々な売り文句がハイクオリティかつハイセンスで表示されている。

実際の駅弁売り場に並んでいそうなデザイン
キャラクターを「食」をテーマにデフォルメしたイラスト
色数は抑えめで、食品表示・ロゴ・キャッチコピー風のレイアウト
参考画像と弁当のコンセプトを大げさに反映した価格を表示する。

キャラクター性を活かたユーモラスな商品名が入っている
冒頭のキャラクター名が設定してある場合はそれを使う
印刷の光沢、紙の厚み、折り返し部分もリアルに描写
※この蓋は中身のコンセプトと強く連動している。
（構図・撮影スタイル）
テーブルの上に置かれた弁当を、**やや斜め上からの真俯瞰寄り（商品撮影的フラットレイ）**で撮影。

8K解像度、超写実的なフードフォト。

「コンビニ・デパ地下・駅弁フェア」に並んでいても違和感のないクオリティ。
（容器 - 弁当箱）
量産品らしい実在感のある弁当箱。

黒・白・木目調など、一般的な弁当容器
仕切り付き、または一体型
角の丸み、成形跡、フチの影までリアル

キャラクター表現の基本構造
顔・身体：

立体的に握られたご飯（白米／炊き込み／混ぜご飯など、コンセプトに応じて変化）
表情・輪郭：

海苔・塩昆布・胡麻・揚げパスタ・刻み野菜などで立体的に表現
コンセプト別おかず展開
参考画像の特徴を誇張したコンセプトにする。
固定メニューではなく、キャラクターや世界観に合わせて自由に変化する。
おかずはすべて実在の食材・調理法のみで構成され、

一つ一つがしっかり立体感と質感を持つ。
（色彩設計）
参照画像の色は直接使わず、
食材として自然な色のみで翻訳。
米の白・薄茶
揚げ物のきつね色
野菜の緑
トマト・梅・人参の赤
卵の黄色
海苔・胡麻の黒
「色分け」ではなく
質感・形・配置の差でキャラクターを認識させる設計。
（文字・ロゴ表現：売り物感の強化）
弁当内の空きスペースに、商品名やキャッチコピーを食材で立体表現。

参考画像の特徴を誇張したものにする。
文字も完全に“食べられるもの”で構成されている。
（背景・環境）
屋外をランダムで選定
サイドからの自然光
唐揚げの油の照り、ご飯の湿り気、野菜の瑞々しさが強調される
全体は温かみのある色温度で、売り場で一番おいしそうに見える光
（全体トーン）
「かわいい」＋「本当に売っていそう」
キャラ弁 × 商品写真 × フードシズルの融合。
```

[[Flat Lay Photography]] [[Packaging Design]]

### 114. 杂乱车库中闪光灯下的街头服饰肖像

**Author**: [Dr. Samia](https://x.com/oye_samia)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张写实风格、全身的年轻女性肖像，她身着垃圾摇滚/街头服饰，坐在一辆红色跑车前，背景是一个杂乱的汽车修理厂。该提示强调了她坚忍的表情、具体的服装细节（超大号的“Chicago”T恤、印花牛仔裤），并使用刺眼、直接的机顶闪光灯照明，营造出一种抓拍、原始的快照感。

```
Framing & Composition
A full-body shot taken from a slightly high angle, looking down at the subject sitting on a concrete garage floor. The subject is centrally framed, positioned directly in front of the hood of a low-profile red sports car. The composition captures the immediacy of a candid snapshot, framing both the subject and the front fascia of the vehicle dominantly.

        "black beanie worn snug",

      ],
      "style_reference": "early-2000s streetwear with modern urban twist"
    }

### 132. 超逼真赛博朋克动作肖像

**Author**: [ぴょんきち|AI兄さん](https://x.com/yarakashiyama_)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的电影级提示，用于生成一张超现实、8K 画质的日本女性动作肖像，背景设定在赛博朋克风格的东京，灵感来源于《黑客帝国》。该提示详细说明了构图（低角度特写）、灯光（翠绿色和金色霓虹灯）以及环境细节（雨水、飞溅的碎片、霓虹灯招牌），以营造一个充满活力的高速动作场景。

```
超リアルな表現、8Kクオリティ。 映画のワンシーンのようなアクションポートレート。 フォーマットは {argument name="画像フォーマット" default="1200×1600 の縦構図"}。 主人公は {argument name="主人公の特徴" default="黒髪ショートボブの日本人女性"}。 参考画像をもとに、顔立ち、表情、体型、全体の雰囲気を正確に再現する。 構図 ローアングルのダイナミックなクローズアップ。 カメラはわずかに見上げる角度で、 彼女が走っている、もしくは跳躍している瞬間を捉えている。 身体は斜めに傾き、右手をカメラに向かって伸ばし、 強い奥行きとスピード感を生み出している。 背景 世界観は「マトリックス」にインスパイアされた美学を固定。 舞台は日本の夜の都市。 雨に濡れた東京の街並みや高架道路、ビル群、漢字やカタカナのネオンサインが並ぶ。 ネオンの色は {argument name="ネオンの色" default="エメラルドグリーンとゴールド"}を基調とし、 未来的でサイバーパンクな雰囲気。 激しい雨が斜めに降り注ぎ、 背景では、超常的な力や衝撃波によって、車や瓦礫が宙に浮いている。 照明 グリーンとゴールドを中心とした照明設計。 冷たい未来的な光と、建物や看板からの温かみのある反射光が混ざり合う。 日本のネオン看板や窓からの光がキーライトとなり、顔の一部を照らす。 背後からの強いグリーンのバックライトがシルエットを際立たせ、 濡れたアスファルトや道路の反射が映画的な奥行きを加えている。 アートディレクション 黒のレザートレンチコートに黒を基調とした衣装。 ネオスタイルの長方形サングラスを着用。 表情は鋭く集中しており、圧倒的な力と意志を感じさせる。 雨、水しぶき、舞い上がる破片、斜めの構図が、 ハイスピードアクションが一瞬で凍りついたような緊張感を生み出す。 ビジュアルスタイル マトリックス的美学。 高コントラスト、精密なテクスチャ、映画的なカラーグレーディング。 24mmレンズ、f/2.8。 高速シャッターで雨と動きを捉え、低ISOでシャープな描写。 ムード 英雄的で、強烈、そして壮大。 まるで彼女が、日本の街を舞台に、 デジタルな戦場で物理法則を超えて戦っているかのような雰囲気。 テキスト、ロゴ、UI、オーバーレイは一切なし。
```

[[Low Angle Close-Up]]

### 133. VTuber 周程表模板

**Author**: [ひいらぎまる](https://x.com/hiiragimaruru)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，用于创建一个干净、扁平、可爱的马卡龙色系周日程表模板，适用于 VTuber 和主播。它包括具体的布局说明、尺寸规格（1920x1080，16:9），以及关于文本内容和为后续角色合成预留空白区域的严格规定。

![VTuber 周程表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468609160_85lvra_G-lyvW7bYAAmJxG.jpg)

```
VTuber・配信者向けの「週間スケジュール」テンプレート画像を作成してください。
横長 16:9、サイズは 1920×1080、フラットで印刷物のように整ったデザイン（ベクター風）。全体はかわいいパステル調（淡いピンク・ミント・ラベンダーのやさしい配色）、でもゴチャつかず見やすさ最優先。

レイアウト指定：
・画面左 60% にスケジュール欄を上寄せで配置。
・7行（曜日は「月・火・水・木・金・土・日」）。
・各行は「曜日ラベル（小さな丸いバッジ）」＋「予定を書き込むための横長の空白ボックス」。
・空白ボックスの中は完全に空欄。サンプル文字（例：ここに予定、SAMPLE、MEMO 等）は絶対に入れない。
・画面右 40% は立ち絵を後から合成できる空きスペース。人物・動物・マスコット・シルエットは描かない。背景は淡いグラデーションと控えめな小さな星/ハート/ドットの抽象パターンのみ。

文字指定：
・入れる文字は「週間スケジュール」と「月 火 水 木 金 土 日」のみ（日本語）。
・それ以外の文字（SNS、日付範囲、注意書き、ロゴ、ハッシュタグ、ウォーターマーク）は一切入れない。
・文字は丸ゴシック風で読みやすく、白背景でも潰れない。

仕上げ：
・余白は外周にしっかり取り、左右の要素が重ならない。
・ロゴなし。
```

[[Kawaii Aesthetic]]

### 139. 编辑平铺时尚图片生成器

**Author**: [Aimi Kōda](https://x.com/aimikoda)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: en

> 一个高度受限的提示模板，旨在生成高分辨率、具有编辑风格的平铺时尚图像，严格采用俯视视角，纯粹专注于服装排列，不描绘或暗示任何人体或体积。

![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900552_gokym2_G-k7N_aW8AA2kuf.jpg)
![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900638_xtp8pr_G-k7MC1WIAIruWa.jpg)
![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900934_thdzb4_G-k7M47X0AEGCba.jpg)

```
[OUTFIT_STYLE] = Use the outfit from the reference image | casual utilitarian womenswear | casual mens streetwear
[COMPOSITION_SCHEME] = seated-inspired angular layout | standing-inspired vertical layout | walking-inspired offset layout | dynamic diagonal layout | balance-inspired asymmetric layout | editorial flat-lay grid break | sculptural negative-space layout | yoga-inspired angular balance layout | athletic-inspired directional layout
[SURFACE] = clean matte studio backdrop | soft neutral paper surface | cool tone matte backdrop
[ACCESSORY_MODE] = outfit_integrated | decorative | none

Make a high resolution flat lay fashion image for editorial and catalog use.
Use a strict top down camera angle with a natural 50mm equivalent perspective and perfectly parallel framing.
Set the scene on [SURFACE] with no visible texture seams or edge shadows.

Show only clothing items and approved accessories placed on the surface.
Do not depict or imply any human body, body parts, limbs, skin, joints, or anatomy.
Do not include legs, hips, feet, knees, or any biological structure.

Arrange garments as a flat, uninhabited composition following [COMPOSITION_SCHEME].
Interpret [COMPOSITION_SCHEME] purely as a geometric layout logic, never as a body configuration.
Use angles, spacing, and directional alignment only to suggest balance and posture.

Keep every garment fully flat with zero internal volume.
Force all bottom garments including pants or leggings to remain collapsed, empty, and tension-free.
Do not stretch, contour, wrap, or compress fabric.
Represent bends only through sharp planar folds and angular breaks.
Prohibit smooth curves, rounded forms, seated volume, or body-fit deformation.

Allow folds and wrinkles only as gravity-driven surface creases.
Ensure clothing reads strictly as laid fabric, not worn, inhabited, or shaped by a body.

Select garments and accessories based on {argument name="outfit style" default="OUTFIT_STYLE"}.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is outfit_integrated, include only functionally worn items.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is decorative, allow accessories as independent flat objects.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is none, exclude all accessories entirely.

Use soft diffused daylight from above with gentle shadows directly beneath each item.
Keep spacing balanced with visible negative space around the composition.
Avoid mannequins, models, body silhouettes, stuffing, air filled shapes, extra items, text, logos, or branding.
Ensure clarity, accurate fabric texture, and a calm contemporary aesthetic.
```

### 146. 音乐策展：为 Pink Floyd 乐迷打造的视听立体模型

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: en

> 这是一个复杂的多步骤提示，旨在充当音乐历史学家和舞台设计师。它分析给定乐队（默认为 Pink Floyd）的音效特征，并生成四个超现实的微缩 2x2 网格立体模型，代表其他乐队的“沧海遗珠”专辑，将其声音转化为建立在旋转黑胶唱片上的实体超现实建筑。

![音乐策展：为 Pink Floyd 乐迷打造的视听立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466893523_jdhs50_G-RllH-W0AAgN-k.jpg)

```
Do this for {argument name="input band" default="Pink Floyd"}: Input Variable: [INSERT BAND/ALBUM] (e.g., Pink Floyd, Daft Punk, Nirvana)
System Instruction:
Act as a Music Historian and Set Designer. Create a 2x2 Grid of "Audio-Visual Dioramas."
1. The Curation Logic (The Deep Cuts):
Analyze Input: Identify the genre and sonic signature of the Input Band.
Select 4 Hidden Gems: Identify 4 lesser-known albums from other bands that share this sonic DNA but offer a different visual flavor.
The Translation: For each album, define the "Sonic Materiality":
If Heavy Metal: Rusty Iron, Fire, Spikes.
If Synth-Pop: Neon Glass, Chrome, Laser Grids.
If Folk/Acoustic: Mossy Wood, Stone, Candlelight.
If Prog Rock: Surreal Marble, Floating Prisms, Clouds.
2. The "Immutable" Container (The Vinyl Stage):
The Base: Each diorama is built on top of a Spinning Vinyl Record acting as the circular stage floor.
The Plinth: The record sits on a high-end, thick Audiophile Turntable Base (Wood or Brushed Aluminum).
The Nameplate (CRITICAL TEXT FIX): On the vertical front face of the Plinth, there is a Polished Brass or Digital Display Plate.
Text Rule: It must clearly display the [ARTIST NAME] in bold, legible, capital letters.
3. The Composition (The Sound Made Solid):
CRITICAL: Do not just recreate the album cover. Build a world that feels like the music.
The Structure: Architecture rises from the grooves of the vinyl record.
Example: A wall of amplifiers, a surreal floating prism, a crumbling brick wall, or a forest of microphone stands.
The Atmosphere: Use particle effects to visualize the sound waves.
Visuals: Floating musical notes made of smoke, vibrating liquid surfaces, or shattered glass suspended in mid-air.
The Figures: Tiny 1:87 scale band members performing inside this surreal landscape.
4. Visual Syntax (Per Panel):
Panel A: Album 1 (Focus on Surrealism/Scale).
Panel B: Album 2 (Focus on Technology/Machinery).
Panel C: Album 3 (Focus on Nature/Organic Textures).
Panel D: Album 4 (Focus on Light/Color).
5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Concert Lighting: Each box is lit like a stage show. Spotlights, laser beams, and stage haze.
Depth: Shallow depth of field (Tilt-Shift) to make the vinyl record look massive.
Background: Seamless Slate Grey to keep the focus on the colors.
Output: 2x2 Grid, Hyper-Realistic Miniature Set Design, 8k Resolution, "Audiophile" Aesthetic.
```

[[Surreal Architecture]]

### 166. 动态流体排版汽水广告提示

**Author**: [Mo](https://x.com/Kerroudjm)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: en

### 176. 美食视频的神奇转换提示词编译器（系统提示）

**Author**: [Emily](https://x.com/IamEmily2050)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: en

> 一个高度复杂、多层次的系统提示，被设计为“魔法转换提示编译器”，用于生成 AI 驱动的食物转换视频。它概述了核心原则，例如关注点分离、像素主权（定义锁定区、转换区和瞬态区），以及体积和状态变化的物理合理性规则。这是一个元提示结构，旨在指导为各种图像和视频模型的多阶段工作流生成特定的机器提示。

```
# MAGICAL TRANSFORMATION PROMPT COMPILER v4.0 (Part 1 of 2)
# Production-Grade Latent Trajectory Generator

system_identity:
  name: "Magical Transformation Prompt Compiler"
  version: "4.0"
  role: >
    You are a precision prompt architect for AI-generated food transformation videos. 
    You produce complete, production-ready specification documents that include operator 
    instructions, machine prompts, and failure suppression layers. Your outputs are used 
    by professional AI artists running multi-stage workflows across image generators 
    (Midjourney, DALL-E, Flux) and video models (Veo3, Kling, Runway).

# CORE PRINCIPLES
core_principles:
  separation_of_concerns:
    description: "Distinct output types for different consumers"
    layers:
      - name: "OPERATOR INSTRUCTIONS"
        purpose: "Human-readable workflow guidance"
        format: "Step-by-step procedural text"
      - name: "MACHINE PROMPTS"
        purpose: "Copy-paste ready AI prompts"
        format: "Quoted prompt blocks with **PROMPT:** prefix"
      - name: "NEGATIVE PROMPTS"
        purpose: "Failure mode suppression"
        format: "Comma-separated exclusion terms"

  pixel_sovereignty:
    description: "Every pixel belongs to exactly ONE zone"
    zones:
      - name: "LOCKED"
        definition: "Immutable across all frames"
        examples: ["table surface", "container exterior", "shadows", "frame edges"]
      - name: "TRANSFORM"
        definition: "Changes between Frame A and Frame B"
        examples: ["container interior", "ingredients", "liquid level"]
      - name: "TRANSIENT"
        definition: "Exists only in video bridge"
        examples: ["motion blur", "steam during reveal", "hand movement"]

  physical_plausibility:
    description: "Transformations must obey observable physics"
    rules:
      - "Volume conservation with specified percentage change"
      - "Mass-energy consistency (cooking typically reduces volume)"
      - "Gravity compliance (no floating elements)"
      - "Temporal logic (effects follow causes, never precede)"
      - "State changes must be chemically plausible"

# INPUT SCHEMA
input_schema:
  required_parameters:
    concept:
      type: "string"
      description: "Name of the dish or transformation"
      examples: ["Beef Bourguignon", "Sushi Platter", "Korean Army Stew"]

  optional_parameters:
    cuisine_context:
      cuisine_origin:
        type: "string"
        description: "Cultural origin informing aesthetic defaults"
        examples: ["French", "Japanese", "Korean", "Italian", "Mexican"]
        inference_rule: "If not provided, infer from concept name"
      
      cooking_method:
        type: "string"
        description: "Primary cooking technique"
        examples: ["braised", "grilled", "fried", "steamed", "raw assembly"]
        inference_rule: "Infer from concept if not specified"

    transform_class:
      type: "enu
```

### 178. 大师级道具制作师立体书透视模型生成器

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的系统指令提示，旨在根据用户提供的电影或书籍名称，生成一个超现实的、微距摄影风格的立体书微缩模型场景。该指令要求 AI 分析源材料的生物群落、冲突、载具和物质性，以构建场景。

![大师级道具制作师立体书透视模型生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768467021160_zumxv2_G-bzqD1WMAEn1k3.jpg)

```
Do it for Terminator: {argument name="title" default="Moby Dick"}

System Instruction:
Act as a Master Prop Maker. Generate a hyper-realistic, macro-photography shot of a "Pop-Up Book Diorama."
1. Forensic Analysis:
Analyze the Input Title to determine the visual components:
The Biome: Identify the primary setting (e.g., Ocean, Jungle, Space, Desert).
The Conflict: Identify the Antagonist or Monster (e.g., The White Whale, T-Rex, Darth Vader).
The Vessel/Hero: Identify the main vehicle or protagonist (e.g., The Pequod, The Jeep, The Millennium Falcon).
The Materiality: Identify the texture of the world (e.g., Wood & Water; Amber & Leaf; Metal & Stars).
2.  Container (The Open Book):
The Object: A massive, vintage, leather-bound hardcover book lying flat on a wooden desk.
The Transformation: The book is open to the middle. The pages do not just lie flat; they physically mutate into the "Biome" identified in Step 1.
Example: If Ocean, the pages turn into turbulent resin waves. If Desert, they turn into dunes.
3. Typography (The Floating Title):
The Text: The [Title of the Input] rises out of the landscape as massive, 3D block letters.
Integration: The letters must interact with the environment.
Texture: The letters are made of materials from the story (e.g., Driftwood, Stone, Bone).
Placement: The waves crash over the letters; vines wrap around the letters.
4. The Action Scene :
CRITICAL: Construct a specific scene using miniature models on top of the book.
The Threat: Place the "Antagonist" looming large in the background (e.g., The Whale breaching behind the text).
The Hero: Place the "Vessel" or "Protagonist" navigating the terrain in the foreground (e.g., A tiny ship rocking on the waves).
Scale: The scene must look like a high-end model kit (1:87 scale).
5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
The Lamp: A vintage brass desk lamp is visible in the corner, casting a warm, directional "reading light" onto the scene.
Atmosphere: Magical realism. The water should glisten; the fog should swirl.
Depth: Shallow depth of field to blur the edge of the desk, keeping focus on the book.
Output: ONE image, 16:9 Aspect Ratio, Cinematic Miniature Photography, 8k Resolution.
```

[[Miniature Scene]] [[Surreal Architecture]] [[Macro Photography Style]]

### 182. 自拍人像冷暖光对比

**Author**: [行者AI视频](https://x.com/joshesye)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作的年轻亚洲女性的垂直特写自拍肖像。该提示强调了具体的发型、妆容、服装和配饰细节，并着重于戏剧性的光线对比——主体上的冷蓝色/紫色光线和背景中的暖黄色钨丝灯光——以实现逼真的社交媒体风格“自拍”美学。

![自拍人像冷暖光对比](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768379509197_ybmo8o_G-jOkfSbcAA_kdf.jpg)

```
【主题】一位年轻女性，深棕黑色头发盘成发髻，额前散落几缕碎刘海；直视镜头，表情宁静略带慵懒。右手托腮，左手持手机作自拍姿势。

【妆容与肤质】自然清透妆容，眼妆干净，睫毛根根分明，双唇莹润；皮肤极其细腻，整体肤色在冷光映衬下透出蓝紫色光泽感。

【衣着】白色细吊带低胸上衣（简约修身款）。

【配饰】手腕叠戴透明粉珠串手链与金色细链手镯（带小花/四叶草吊坠）；指甲涂浅裸色甲油。

【道具】亮黄色手机/手机壳非常醒目（位于画面左下角），增强“随手社交自拍”的真实感。

【场景】昏暗餐厅/酒吧氛围，厚重黑窗帘为背景；白色圆桌上放置酒杯与小物件，多盏暖黄色台灯营造温馨环境光。

【光影与色彩】人物受冷蓝紫色补光（如屏幕光/LED补光）照射，背景则泛暖黄色钨丝灯光，形成鲜明冷暖对比；背景轻微虚化以突出人像。

【摄影语言】竖构图近景半身（胸部以上），略带俯视/平视角度，带手机人像模式质感，中浅景深，画面肌理“清晰而柔和”。
```

[[Asian Female Portrait]]

### 191. Liquid Glass UX 按钮提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro

The lighting is soft and even, resembling indoor natural light or softbox lighting, giving the skin a delicate texture. There is a black hair tie on her wrist (adding a touch of realistic detail). ### 199. 简化版对比信息图网格生成器提示（腿部和丝袜）

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2026-01-13  **Language**: zh

3.  **Photography Style:** Clean, controlled studio photography with neutral, even lighting designed to highlight texture differences.

(AI Instructions: First, check the value of User Input Setting "# 4. Show Text Overlay at Bottom". You MUST execute ONLY ONE of the following logic blocks based on that value.)

##### ➤ LOGIC PATH A: IF Setting #4 is "Yes" (Show Overlay)
If the user selected "Yes", EVERY panel must feature a precisely designed text overlay at the bottom following these strict rules:
* **Background:** A clean, sharply defined solid rectangular color block (e.g., charcoal grey or black) spanning the entire width of the panel's bottom section.
* **Typography:** Inside this block, the text must be rendered in an **elegant, ultra-thin, minimalist sans-serif font**.
* **Layout:** The text "[Number]. [Short Title] (Prompt: [Key English Prompt Snippet])" must be perfectly centered within the color block.
* **Aesthetic:** The overall effect should be that of professional, minimalist graphic design, with crisp lines and perfect alignment.

##### ➤ LOGIC PATH B: IF Setting #4 is "No" (Hide Overlay)
If the user selected "No", apply this CRITICAL rule:
* **CRITICAL:** DO NOT add any text overlay, numbers, titles, background color blocks, or prompt snippets to the images.
* **Result:** The bottom of every panel must be clean image data only, showing the subject fully without obstruction.

# Base Subject Definition:
The base scene for every panel is: **[Insert description from "2. Base Subject Description" here]**. The variations below will modify the surface or appearance of this base subject.

# Variations Data List (Apply sequentially to the grid):
(AI instructions: Iterate through this list based on the required grid size. For each panel, apply the user-defined 'Visual Change' to the base
```
